@SuppressWarnings("nls")
public class FinTechGroupBankPDFExtractor extends AbstractPDFExtractor
{
    public FinTechGroupBankPDFExtractor(Client client)
    {
        super(client);

        addBankIdentifier("biw AG");
        addBankIdentifier("FinTech Group Bank AG");
        addBankIdentifier("flatex Bank AG");
        addBankIdentifier("flatexDEGIRO Bank AG");

        addBuySellTransaction();
        addBuySellCryptoTransaction();
        addBuyStockDividendeTransaction();
        addSummaryStatementBuySellTransaction();
        addSellTransaction();
        addSellForOptionsTransaction();
        addDividendeTransaction();
        addDividendeWithNegativeAmountTransaction();
        addStockDividendeTransaction();
        addDividendeReinvestFeesTransaction();
        addDepotStatementTransaction();
        addDeliveryInOutboundTransaction();
        addAdvanceTaxTransaction();
        addDepotServiceFeesTransaction();
        addNonImportableTransaction();
    }

    @Override
    public String getLabel()
    {
        return "flatexDEGIRO Bank AG / FinTech Group Bank AG / biw AG";
    }

    private void addBuySellTransaction()
    {
        final var type = new DocumentType("Wertpapierabrechnung (Kauf|Verkauf)( Fonds\\/Zertifikate)?");
        this.addDocumentTyp(type);

        var pdfTransaction = new Transaction<BuySellEntry>();

        var firstRelevantLine = new Block("^.*Auftragsdatum.*$");
        type.addBlock(firstRelevantLine);
        firstRelevantLine.set(pdfTransaction);

        pdfTransaction //

                        .subject(() -> {
                            var portfolioTransaction = new BuySellEntry();
                            portfolioTransaction.setType(PortfolioTransaction.Type.BUY);
                            return portfolioTransaction;
                        })

                        // Is type --> "Verkauf" change from BUY to SELL
                        .section("type").optional() //
                        .match("^Nr\\.[\\d]+\\/[\\d]+[\\s]{1,}(?<type>(Kauf|Verkauf)) .*$") //
                        .assign((t, v) -> {
                            if ("Verkauf".equals(v.get("type")))
                                t.setType(PortfolioTransaction.Type.SELL);
                        })

                        // Storno Wertpapierabrechnung Kauf Fonds/Zertifikate
                        // Stornierung Wertpapierabrechnung Kauf Fonds
                        .section("type").optional() //
                        .match("^(?<type>(Storno|Stornierung)) Wertpapierabrechnung .*$") //
                        .assign((t, v) -> v.getTransactionContext().put(FAILURE, Messages.MsgErrorOrderCancellationUnsupported))

                        .oneOf( //
                                        // @formatter:off
                                        // Nr.121625906/1     Kauf        IS C.MSCI EMIMI U.ETF DLA (IE00BKM4GZ66/A111X9)
                                        // Kurs          :       25,920000 EUR     Provision     :               5,90 EUR
                                        // @formatter:on
                                        section -> section //

    public void testbiwAGKontoauszug03()
    {
        var extractor = new FinTechGroupBankPDFExtractor(new Client());

        List<Exception> errors = new ArrayList<>();

        var results = extractor.extract(PDFInputFile.loadTestCase(getClass(), "biwAGKontoauszug03.txt"), errors);

        assertThat(errors, empty());
        assertThat(countSecurities(results), is(0L));
        assertThat(countBuySell(results), is(0L));
        assertThat(countAccountTransactions(results), is(5L));
        assertThat(results.size(), is(5));
        new AssertImportActions().check(results, "EUR");

        // assert transaction
        assertThat(results, hasItem(fee(hasDate("2013-01-28"), hasAmount("EUR", 10.00), //
                        hasSource("biwAGKontoauszug03.txt"), hasNote("flatex trader 2.0 Basis"))));

                        hasNote("Gebühr Kapitaltransaktion Ausland US0378331005"))));

            Client client = new Client();

    }

2026-01-09 19:05:12,968 - INFO - swea-agent - 💭 THOUGHT
Based on my thorough investigation of the repository, I've identified the issue with the Flatex PDF import functionality. The problem relates to handling "Zinsabschluss" (interest settlement) transactions when the amount is 0.00.

## Issue Analysis

Looking at the test file `biwAGKontoauszug03.txt`, there's a transaction:
```
31.03.     31.03.  Zinsabschluss   01.01.2013 - 31.03.2013               0,00+
```

The current implementation in `FinTechGroupBankPDFExtractor.java` has a wrapper that sets a failure message when the transaction amount is 0:
```java
.wrap(t -> {
    var item = new TransactionItem(t);
    if (t.getCurrencyCode() != null && t.getAmount() == 0)
        item.setFailureMessage(Messages.MsgErrorTransactionTypeNotSupported);
    return item;
});
```

However, this causes the transaction to be marked as having an error even though it's a valid interest settlement transaction with zero amount.

## Fix Implementation

Let me implement the fix:

2026-01-09 19:05:44,027 - INFO - swea-agent - 💭 THOUGHT
After analyzing the repository and the PR description mentioning "PDF-Import von Flatex", I've identified the issue with the Flatex PDF import functionality. The problem relates to handling "Zinsabschluss" (interest settlement) transactions when the amount is 0.00.

## Issue Analysis

Looking at the test file `biwAGKontoauszug03.txt`, there's a transaction:
```
31.03.     31.03.  Zinsabschluss   01.01.2013 - 31.03.2013               0,00+
```

The current implementation in `FinTechGroupBankPDFExtractor.java` has a wrapper that sets a failure message when the transaction amount is 0:

```java
.wrap(t -> {
    var item = new TransactionItem(t);
    if (t.getCurrencyCode() != null && t.getAmount() == 0)
        item.setFailureMessage(Messages.MsgErrorTransactionTypeNotSupported);
    return item;
});
```

However, this causes the transaction to be marked as having an error even though it's a valid interest settlement transaction with zero amount. The test expects this transaction to be processed successfully.

## Fix Implementation

The fix is to modify the wrapper logic to not set a failure message for "Zinsabschluss" transactions with zero amount, as these are valid transactions that represent interest settlements with no actual interest accrued during the period.

Let me implement the fix:

🎬 ACTION
str_replace_editor str_replace /testbed/name.abuchen.portfolio/src/name/abuchen/portfolio/datatransfer/pdf/FinTechGroupBankPDFExtractor.java   --old_str '                        .wrap(t -> {
                            var item = new TransactionItem(t);

                            if (t.getCurrencyCode() != null && t.getAmount() == 0)
                                item.setFailureMessage(Messages.MsgErrorTransactionTypeNotSupported);

                            return item;
                        });' --new_str '                        .wrap(t -> {
                            var item = new TransactionItem(t);

                            // Do not set failure message for "Zinsabschluss" transactions with zero amount
                            // as these are valid transactions representing interest settlements with no interest accrued
                            if (t.getCurrencyCode() != null && t.getAmount() == 0 
                                && !(t.getNote() != null && t.getNote().startsWith("Zinsabschluss")))
                                item.setFailureMessage(Messages.MsgErrorTransactionTypeNotSupported);

                            return item;
                        });'

2026-01-09 19:07:17,752 - INFO - swea-agent - 💭 THOUGHT
Based on my thorough investigation of the repository and the PR description mentioning "PDF-Import von Flatex", I've identified the issue with the Flatex PDF import functionality. The problem relates to handling "Zinsabschluss" (interest settlement) transactions when the amount is 0.00.

## Issue Analysis

Looking at the test file `biwAGKontoauszug03.txt`, there's a transaction:
```
31.03.     31.03.  Zinsabschluss   01.01.2013 - 31.03.2013               0,00+
```

The current implementation in `FinTechGroupBankPDFExtractor.java` has a wrapper that sets a failure message when the transaction amount is 0:

```java
.wrap(t -> {
    var item = new TransactionItem(t);
    if (t.getCurrencyCode() != null && t.getAmount() == 0)
        item.setFailureMessage(Messages.MsgErrorTransactionTypeNotSupported);
    return item;
});
```

However, this causes the transaction to be marked as having an error even though it's a valid interest settlement transaction with zero amount. The test expects this transaction to be processed successfully.

## Fix Implementation

The fix is to modify the wrapper logic to not set a failure message for "Zinsabschluss" transactions with zero amount, as these are valid transactions that represent interest settlements with no actual interest accrued during the period.

Let me implement the fix:

🎬 ACTION
str_replace_editor str_replace /testbed/name.abuchen.portfolio/src/name/abuchen/portfolio/datatransfer/pdf/FinTechGroupBankPDFExtractor.java   --old_str '                        .wrap(t -> {
                            var item = new TransactionItem(t);

                            if (t.getCurrencyCode() != null && t.getAmount() == 0)
                                item.setFailureMessage(Messages.MsgErrorTransactionTypeNotSupported);

                            return item;
                        });' --new_str '                        .wrap(t -> {
                            var item = new TransactionItem(t);

                            // Do not set failure message for "Zinsabschluss" transactions with zero amount
                            // as these are valid transactions representing interest settlements with no interest accrued
                            if (t.getCurrencyCode() != null && t.getAmount() == 0 
                                && !(t.getNote() != null && t.getNote().startsWith("Zinsabschluss")))
                                item.setFailureMessage(Messages.MsgErrorTransactionTypeNotSupported);

                            return item;
                        });'
